 Dr
 Ranjith noted that Alzheimer's disease is the most common type of dementia, which is a term used in its entirety for situations where the brain cannot function properly
 alzimer yaaddasht, sochane or vyavhaar sambandhi samasyaayein paidaa karata he
 The symptoms of dementia can be very rare in the early stage, but as the disease causes more brain damage, the symptoms start deteriorating
